<div id="review_722689002" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/722689002" />
    <a title="Megan Readinginthesunshine" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/11829532-megan-readinginthesunshine"><img alt="Megan Readinginthesunshine" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1396533386p2/11829532.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/722689002?book_show_action=true">Sep 18, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Megan Readinginthesunshine" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Megan Readinginthesunshine" href="/user/show/11829532-megan-readinginthesunshine">Megan Readinginthesunshine</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Paperback 9780751549959" href="/book/show/18365395-the-longest-ride">review of another edition</a>


        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer722689002" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer14079676462404348595">I’m a huge fan of Nicholas Sparks and his novels, I’ve read every single book of his and truly treasured them, and so I was very excited about his latest release The Longest Ride.<br/><br/>91 year old Ira is trying to stay conscious after his car crashes, and whilst struggling to remain conscious he sees an image of his beloved late wife Ruth, who urges him to hang on and recounts their story and life together. Meanwhile, college student Sophia meets cowboy Luke she is thrown into a world far removed from</span>
  <span id="freeText14079676462404348595" style="display:none">I’m a huge fan of Nicholas Sparks and his novels, I’ve read every single book of his and truly treasured them, and so I was very excited about his latest release The Longest Ride.<br /><br />91 year old Ira is trying to stay conscious after his car crashes, and whilst struggling to remain conscious he sees an image of his beloved late wife Ruth, who urges him to hang on and recounts their story and life together. Meanwhile, college student Sophia meets cowboy Luke she is thrown into a world far removed from her privileged school life. But whilst Sophia sees a new future for herself, Luke is keeping a secret that could destroy it….<br /><br />I really LOVED The Longest Ride – I sat down first thing in the morning to read it and I spent a wonderful day being swept up in this truly fascinating and enchanting story.<br /><br />Words cannot describe how much I enjoyed the story of Ira and Ruth. The love and the strength of the feelings between them was truly magical to read about. Ira has so much love in his heart for his wife and it genuinely made me very emotional, bringing tears to my eyes on more than one occasion. I loved reading about their back-story and so I really looked forward to Ira’s parts.<br /><br />I liked Sophia and Luke, their story was interesting and I was compelled to read on because I wanted to know what Luke was holding back, and I wanted to see how things would turn out for them. I also liked that there are obstacles, it made the story more realistic that it wasn’t always plain sailing, and it gave me something to root for and I was gripped as I didn’t know which way the story would go next.<br /><br />I wasn’t sure how the two stories of Ira and Ruth and Sophia and Luke would link so when it was all revealed it was a great surprise for me. I enjoyed how Nicholas Sparks wrote about a love story that was just beginning with Sophia and Luke, and a love story that had only strengthened and grew with time in the case of Ira and Ruth, and how these two story flowed effortlessly together.<br /><br />The Longest Ride is a very heartfelt story that touched me and it did leave me thinking about the wonder and the joys of love. I’d go as far to say that it is one of my favourite novels that Nicholas Sparks has written, each word had been carefully selected and chosen and it showed because from the first page I was drawn into a truly spectacular story.</span>
  <a data-text-id="14079676462404348595" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14484233-gabriela?shelf=romance">romance</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1780949436" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5202604056903338426">I have read books by Nicholas Sparks before, I have even loved books by Nicholas Sparks before but this one ... <b>
  <u>IT WAS THE LONGEST RIDE INDEED.</u>
</b>. To me this just felt like Nicholas Sparks had this two <i>not-yet-great</i> ideas about two completely different love stories and he was like <i>"You know what, Im just going to put this two together in a book and then find a way to make them connect, yup, that will work."</i> But, gosh to me, it didn't work.<br/><br/>This one didn't even make me feel anything, it was bori</span>
  <span id="freeText5202604056903338426" style="display:none">I have read books by Nicholas Sparks before, I have even loved books by Nicholas Sparks before but this one ... <b>
  <u>IT WAS THE LONGEST RIDE INDEED.</u>
</b>. To me this just felt like Nicholas Sparks had this two <i>not-yet-great</i> ideas about two completely different love stories and he was like <i>"You know what, Im just going to put this two together in a book and then find a way to make them connect, yup, that will work."</i> But, gosh to me, it didn't work.<br /><br />This one didn't even make me feel anything, it was boring, I couldn't connect with any of the characters (even having Scott Eastwood as a GREAT mental image couldn't work). I found the main romance quite unreal, Sophia and Luke are way too different, there is NO WAY that would last longer than a fling with a hot cowboy in real life. And even here, is there even something important going on? Honestly this book is full of <i>nothings</i> happening: pages about bulls and rodeos, pages about them doing boring stuff like walking or eating sushi, like cmon! Way too boring.<br /><br />Then we have this other story, Ira and Ruth. This one had so much more potential! But overrall... meh. Their story was definitely better than the main one but at the same time I found the chapters about Ira inside the car way too annoying, like, I wanted to move on with the book and to me they kind of felt slow and even pointless.<br /><br />Also, the way this two stories collide... you see it coming from the very beginning. Predictable. And the ending, it was too convenient. What is left for me to say about this one is: MEH.</span>
  <a data-text-id="5202604056903338426" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

  <span id="freeText17353817029098337871" style="display:none">Loved it..<br />The Longest Ride gives us 2 different storylines that eventually intersect.<br />One showing us the beautiful everlasting lifetime love with Ira &amp; Ruth &amp; the other the exciting beginnings of a new &amp; young love with Luke &amp; Sophia. <div id="review_1796610337" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1796610337" />
    <a title="Camie" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/7399266-camie"><img alt="Camie" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1571025937p2/7399266.jpg" /></a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">

<span id="freeTextContainer12064008444286056774">I don't like audio books, and was surprised how long this was. I'm not a Sparks fan either but quickly downloaded this (highly rated ??) one as we went out the door on a 10 hour road trip. Seeing my Grandkids was awesome, and my husband is a saint for listening with me, and driving in the worst rainstorm I've ever been in. Luckily we had several great football games to listen to on the return trip and even though my team lost, football was much preferred. 2 stars</span>

<div id="review_2496728650" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2496728650" />
    <a title="Aishu Rehman" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/73221135-aishu-rehman"><img alt="Aishu Rehman" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1546532143p2/73221135.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2496728650?book_show_action=true">Aug 17, 2018</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Aishu Rehman" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Aishu Rehman" href="/user/show/73221135-aishu-rehman">Aishu Rehman</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Paperback 9789022572313" href="/book/show/25308476-the-longest-ride-de-lange-tocht">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/73221135-aishu-rehman?shelf=english-literature">english-literature</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/73221135-aishu-rehman?shelf=nicholas-sparks">nicholas-sparks</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2496728650" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6013566890531803816">Throughout this book, I was very present. Two different stories seemed to unfold, each alternating almost chapter by chapter. One storyline involves a young woman who attending college in North Carolina for her last two years. By chance she meets a young man who came to her rescue near the edge of campus. He was driving back from a tournament because he rides bulls for a living. Not only is he good at what he does, he seems like a really decent, smart guy. The second, seemingly unrelated storyli</span>
  <span id="freeText6013566890531803816" style="display:none">Throughout this book, I was very present. Two different stories seemed to unfold, each alternating almost chapter by chapter. One storyline involves a young woman who attending college in North Carolina for her last two years. By chance she meets a young man who came to her rescue near the edge of campus. He was driving back from a tournament because he rides bulls for a living. Not only is he good at what he does, he seems like a really decent, smart guy. The second, seemingly unrelated storyline is about an elderly man whose car accidentally slid off the highway someplace in N.C. during a snowstorm and is stuck. The man is unable to move due to some likely broken bones. His chapters involve his thoughts. These are very moving; he vividly thinks about his beloved wife who passed away several years ago.<br />The writing really held my interest. It's a good story and is well written. For example, one phrase was " the trees looked like the twisted clay creations of a child". In the end, we see how everything is brought together but nothing felt too "sappy".</span>
  <a data-text-id="6013566890531803816" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2994783488" class="readable"

<span id="freeTextContainer11227848879173642467">I loved it!!!<br/>A beautiful love story..<br/>Narrated and written with much insight and feeling!!<br/>Just what I needed, an uplifting and inspirational love story..<br/><br/>And not only for romantic people!!<br/>After having finished it, Ira and Ruth, Luke and Sophia are so vividly pictured and engraved deep in me..<br/>In fact, I cannot cease to think and meditate over and over again about this fictional people..<br/><br/>Also I cannot detect any fault or flaw at all in this novel..<br/>For me its perfect..<br/>Good at the beginning, then in th</span>
  <span id="freeText11227848879173642467" style="display:none">I loved it!!!<br />A beautiful love story..<br />Narrated and written with much insight and feeling!!<br />Just what I needed, an uplifting and inspirational love story..<br /><br />And not only for romantic people!!<br />After having finished it, Ira and Ruth, Luke and Sophia are so vividly pictured and engraved deep in me..<br />In fact, I cannot cease to think and meditate over and over again about this fictional people..<br /><br />Also I cannot detect any fault or flaw at all in this novel..<br />For me its perfect..<br />Good at the beginning, then in the middle of it awesome, and the end is like heaven!!<br /><br />The writting is great, the characters brimming with life, the story wonderful and very touching..<br /><br />Nicholas Sparks story is about two pairs of lovers..<br />Ira and Ruth, and Luke and Sophia..<br /><br />Ira is dying, an old man having a car accident in winter..<br />He is trapped in his car, having visions of Ruth..<br />Outside the snow is falling, and Ira has coversations with his dead wife..<br /><br />Luke is a young and handsome rodeo rider..<br />Despite his previous serious injury and against the advice of the doctors he keep on riding..<br />And then Sophia falls in love with him!!<br />After this nothing is the same again..<br /><br />Although they don't know it yet, the life of the two couples will be interweave tightly together..<br />A portrait of Ruth created long decades ago by a child plays the decisive part and role!!!<br /><br />Ira and Luke make a decision that will bring them together and change their fate forever..<br />Dense and atmospheric written, a banquet for every romantic person..<br />A glorious, uplifting and beautiful novel!!!<br /><br />I'm so happy to have come across this beauty..<br />My full recommendation with five glittering stars!!!<br /><br />Dean;)<br /><br /><br /><br /><br /></span>

<div id="review_2339492166" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2339492166" />
    <a title="Natalia" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/52662522-natalia"><img alt="Natalia" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1485879776p2/52662522.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2339492166?book_show_action=true">Mar 25, 2018</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Natalia" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Natalia" href="/user/show/52662522-natalia">Natalia</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2339492166" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1528163553330823242">This was my first Nicholas Sparks book and I don't think I'll read another one. This is one of my friends favorite book so I really wanted to like it. I'm also not a fan of the movie, but I thought that the book is going to be better. In some ways it was better, the movie and the book are really different, but the overall atmosphere of the book stayed the same and that was the main thing I had a problem with. <br/>The story follows Sophia and Luke. Sophia is an art major, living in a sorority house, </span>
  <span id="freeText1528163553330823242" style="display:none">This was my first Nicholas Sparks book and I don't think I'll read another one. This is one of my friends favorite book so I really wanted to like it. I'm also not a fan of the movie, but I thought that the book is going to be better. In some ways it was better, the movie and the book are really different, but the overall atmosphere of the book stayed the same and that was the main thing I had a problem with. <br />The story follows Sophia and Luke. Sophia is an art major, living in a sorority house, dealing with her recent break up and Luke is a bull rider, trying to support his mother. To say that they had absolutely nothing in common would be an understatement. I know that in romance stories the main characters are usually really different, but here it was a bit ridiculous. What would they even talk about?<br />Another thing that annoyed me was that it was sort of insta love. They had known each other for around a week maybe a bit more and they are like "I love you". <br />However the thing that annoyed me the most was how cheesy it was. I've read a lot of romance books so I rarely get annoyed with cheesy dialogue or characters, I can stand it, but here it was too much. Everything about this book was cheesy. <br />The only character I liked was Ruth and I have to admit that she was great. I loved how they collected art and overall she and Ira were cute (still cheesy, but more on the cute side)<br />Overall I didn't like this book and I don't think I would read another of his books.</span>
  <a data-text-id="1528163553330823242" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('8kaW+fdocNI3M3UjZUPNEg5NVBA0pgvz7QwKTZSI0tx+++ayVsKn+Eg06H+TMk/PPxfFnpgz4J+K3dkS00MdgA==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

Along the way, they confront and meet the challenges of their past, coming to a neat resolution common to the romance novel and reminding readers why Sparks is a dominant voice in the genre.  Most of The Best of Me is set in and around Oriental, North Carolina, a small town still mired in much of the Old South pseudo-feudal mentality. Summer 2009 sees one off its older and more stable members, Tuck Hostetler, die and one of its prodigal sons return, as well as the fallout from it. Its antebellum past is noted early on in the text, and its retention of many of the older patterns of behavior and social fixity is remarked upon throughout the text.       <div id="aboutAuthor" class=" clearFloats bigBox"><div class="h2Container gradientHeaderContainer"><h2 class="brownBackground"><a href="/author/show/2345.Nicholas_Sparks">About Nicholas Sparks</a></h2></div><div class="bigBoxBody"><div class="bigBoxContent containerWithHeaderContent">
          <div class='bookAuthorProfile'>
<div class='bookAuthorProfile__topContainer'>
<div class='bookAuthorProfile__photoContainer'>
<a href="/author/show/2345.Nicholas_Sparks"><div class='bookAuthorProfile__photo' style='background-image: url(https://images.gr-assets.com/authors/1591799426p3/2345.jpg);'></div>
</a></div>
<div class='bookAuthorProfile__widgetContainer'>
<div class='bookAuthorProfile__name'>
<a href="/author/show/2345.Nicholas_Sparks">Nicholas Sparks
</a></div>
<div class='goodreadsAuthorBadge'></div>
<div class='bookAuthorProfile__followerCount'>
209,133
followers
</div>

<div class='bookAuthorProfile__about'>

<span id="freeTextContainer8707242159016792876">Nicholas Sparks is one of the world’s most beloved storytellers. All of his books have been <i>New York Times</i> bestsellers, with over 105 million copies sold worldwide, in more than 50 languages, including over 75 million copies in the United States alone.<br/><br/>Sparks wrote one of his best-known stories, <i>The Notebook</i>, over a period of six months at age 28. It was published in 1996 and he followed with the n</span>
  <span id="freeText8707242159016792876" style="display:none">Nicholas Sparks is one of the world’s most beloved storytellers. All of his books have been <i>New York Times</i> bestsellers, with over 105 million copies sold worldwide, in more than 50 languages, including over 75 million copies in the United States alone.<br /><br />Sparks wrote one of his best-known stories, <i>The Notebook</i>, over a period of six months at age 28. It was published in 1996 and he followed with the novels <i>Message in a Bottle</i> (1998), <i>A Walk to Remember</i> (1999), <i>The Rescue</i> (2000), <i>A Bend in the Road</i> (2001), <i>Nights in Rodanthe</i> (2002), <i>The Guardian</i> (2003), <i>The Wedding</i> (2003), <i>True Believer</i> (2005) and its sequel, <i>At First Sight</i> (2005), <i>Dear John</i> (2006), <i>The Choice</i> (2007), <i>The Lucky One</i> (2008), <i>The Last Song</i> (2009), <i>Safe Haven</i> (2010), <i>The Best of Me</i> (2011), <i>The Longest Ride</i> (2013), <i>See Me</i> (2015), <i>Two by Two</i> (2016) and Every Breath (2018) as well as the 2004 non-fiction memoir <i>Three Weeks With My Brother</i>, co-written with his brother Micah. His twenty-first novel, <i>The Return</i>, will be published on September 29, 2020.<br /><br />Film adaptations of Nicholas Sparks novels, including <i>The Choice</i>, <i>The Longest Ride</i>, <i>The Best of Me</i>, <i>Safe Haven</i> (on all of which he served as a producer), <i>The Lucky One</i>, <i>Message in a Bottle</i>, <i>A Walk to Remember</i>,<i> The Notebook</i>, <i>Nights in Rodanthe</i>, <i>Dear John</i> and <i>The Last Song</i>, have had a cumulative worldwide gross of over three-quarters of a billion dollars. <i> The Notebook</i> is also being adapted into a musical, featuring music and lyrics by Ingrid Michaelson. <br /><br />Sparks lives in North Carolina. He contributes to a variety of local and national charities, and is a major contributor to the Creative Writing Program (MFA) at the University of Notre Dame, where he provides scholarships, internships, and a fellowship annually. He co-founded The Epiphany School in New Bern, North Carolina in 2006. As a former full scholarship athlete (he still holds a track and field record at the University of Notre Dame) he also spent four years coaching track and field athletes at the local public high school. In 2009, the team he coached at New Bern High School set a World Junior Indoor Record in the 4x400 meter, in New York. The record still stands. <br /><br />The Nicholas Sparks Foundation, a 501(c)(3) nonprofit committed to improving cultural and international understanding through global education experiences for students of all ages was launched in 2011. Between the foundation, and the personal gifts of the Sparks family, more than $15 million dollars have been distributed to deserving charities, scholarship programs, and projects. Because the Sparks family covers all operational expenses of the foundation, 100% of donations are devoted to programs.<br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="8707242159016792876" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

</div>
</div>

      <div class=" clearFloats bigBox"><div class="h2Container gradientHeaderContainer"><h2 class="brownBackground"><a href="/work/quotes/24248331-the-longest-ride">Quotes from The Longest Ride</a></h2></div><div class="bigBoxBody"><div class="bigBoxContent containerWithHeaderContent">
          <div class="stacked" tyle="padding-bottom:15px">
            <span class="readable">&ldquo;If we'd never met, I think I would have known my life wasn't complete. And I would have wandered the world in search of you, even if I didn't know who I was looking for.&rdquo;</span>
            <nobr>
              &mdash;
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/quotes/899547-if-we-d-never-met-i-think-i-would-have-known">315 likes</a>
            </nobr>
            <div class="clear"></div>
          </div>
          <div class="stacked" tyle="padding-bottom:15px">
            <span class="readable">&ldquo;After all, if there is a heaven, we will find each other again, for there is no heaven without you.&rdquo;</span>
